# Tracker: Mailgun

## Disguised trackers list

* mailgun.org
    * email.mailgun.org
    * eu.mailgun.org
    * mxa.mailgun.org
    * smtp.mailgun.org
    * www.mailgun.org
    * xa.mailgun.org

### Rarely active trackers

* email.kdpwizard.app
* email.mg.reframeyourclients.com
* email.catsoneemail.com
* tracking.berserkermail.com
* click.tr.onesignal.email
